<h1 _ngcontent-kva-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.util (util工具函数)"> @ohos.util (util工具函数) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>该模块主要提供常用的工具函数，实现字符串编解码（<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#textencoder">TextEncoder</a>，<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#textdecoder">TextDecoder</a>）、有理数运算（<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#rationalnumber8">RationalNumber<sup>8+</sup></a>）、缓冲区管理（<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#lrucache9">LRUCache<sup>9+</sup></a>）、范围判断（<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#scopehelper9">ScopeHelper<sup>9+</sup></a>）、Base64编解码（<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#base64helper9">Base64Helper<sup>9+</sup></a>）、内置对象类型检查（<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#types8">types<sup>8+</sup></a>）、对方法进行插桩和替换（<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#aspect11">Aspect<sup>11+</sup></a>）等功能。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 7开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3436px;">     <h2 id="utilformat9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">util.format<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="utilformat9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>format(format: string, ...args: Object[]): string</p>     <p>使用样式化字符串将输入内容按特定格式输出。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">format</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">格式化字符串，可以包含零个或多个占位符，用于指定要插入的参数的位置和格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">...args</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Object[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">替换format参数中占位符的数据，此参数缺失时，默认返回第一个参数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">格式化后的字符串。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>格式说明符：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.14.1.3.1.1" width="50%">格式说明符</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.14.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">%s</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">将参数转换为字符串，用于除Object，BigInt和-0之外的所有值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">%d</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">将参数作为十进制整数进行格式化输出，用于除Symbol和BigInt之外的所有值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">%i</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">将字符串转换为十进制整数，用于除BigInt和Symbol之外的所有值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">%f</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">将字符串转换为浮点数，用于除BigInt和Symbol之外的所有值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">%j</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">将JavaScript对象转换为JSON字符串进行格式化输出。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">%o</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">用于将JavaScript对象进行格式化输出，将对象转换为字符串表示，但不包含对象的原型链信息。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">%O</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">用于将JavaScript对象进行格式化输出，将对象转换为字符串表示。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">%c</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">只在浏览器环境中有效。其余环境不会产生样式效果。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">%%</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">转义百分号的特殊格式化占位符。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div homework</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1778px;">     <h2 id="utilerrnotostring9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">util.errnoToString<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>errnoToString(errno: number): string</p>     <p>获取系统错误码对应的详细信息。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">errno</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">系统发生错误产生的错误码。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2.     <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">-5</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">i/o error</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">-11</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">resource temporarily unavailable</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">-12</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">not enough memory</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">-13</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">permission denied</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">-100</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">network is down</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1528px;">     <h2 id="utilcallbackwrapper" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">util.callbackWrapper<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="utilcallbackwrapper" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>callbackWrapper(original: Function): (err: Object, value: Object)=&gt;void</p>     <p>对异步函数进行回调化处理，回调中第一个参数是拒绝原因（如果Promise已解决，则为null），第二个参数是已解决的值。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口要求参数original必须是异步函数类型。如果传入的参数不是异步函数，不会进行拦截，但是会输出错误信息："callbackWrapper: The type of Parameter must be AsyncFunction"。</p>       <p>该接口用于将返回Promise的async函数转换为错误优先回调风格的函数，调用此接口返回的函数接收一个回调函数作为第二个入参，调用此方法时会先执行original函数。当original的Promise返回resolve时，入参的回调函数的第一个参数为null，第二个参数为resolve的值。当original的Promise返回reject时，入参的回调函数的第一个参数为错误对象，第二个参数为null。当original为无入参的函数时，此接口返回的函数第一个入参需传入一个无效的占位参数。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">original</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Function</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">异步函数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">(err: Object, value: Object)=&gt;void</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回一个回调函数，该函数第一个参数err是拒绝原因（如果 Promise 已解决，则为 null），第二个参数value是已解决的值。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="utilpromisify9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1220px;">     <h2 id="utilgeneraterandomuuid9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">util.generateRandomUUID<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="utilgeneraterandomuuid9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>generateRandomUUID(entropyCache?: boolean): string</p>     <p>使用加密安全随机数生成器生成随机的RFC 4122版本4的string类型UUID。为了提升性能，此接口会默认使用缓存，即入参为true，最多可缓存128个随机的UUID。当缓存中128个UUID用尽后，会重新生成，以保证UUID的随机性。如需禁用缓存，请将入参设置为false。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">entropyCache</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是否使用已缓存的UUID，true表示使用缓存的UUID，false表示不使用缓存的UUID，默认true。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.9.1.3.1.1" class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示此UUID的字符串。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1364px;">     <h2 id="utilgethash12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">util.getHash<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="utilgethash12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getHash(object: object): number</p>     <p>获取对象的Hash值。</p>     <p>首次获取时，则计算Hash值并保存到对象的Hash域（返回随机的Hash值）；后续获取时，直接从Hash域中返回Hash值（同一对象多次返回值保持不变）。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">object</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">object</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">需要获取Hash值的对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Hash值。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 778px;">     <h2 id="utilgetmainthreadstacktrace20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">util.getMainThreadStackTrace<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="utilgetmainthreadstacktrace20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getMainThreadStackTrace(): string</p>     <p>获取主线程的栈追踪信息，最多返回64层调用帧。</p>     <p>该接口可能对主线程性能产生影响，建议仅在必要时使用，如日志记录、错误分析或调试场景。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.15.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">主线程的栈追踪信息。若主线程未处于执行JS代码状态，则返回空字符串。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>用于配置decodeToString方法在解码字节流时的行为参数。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 573px;">     <h2 id="decodewithstreamoptions11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">DecodeWithStreamOptions<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="decodewithstreamoptions11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th width="20%">在随后的decodeWithStream()调用中是否跟随附加数据块。如果以块的形式处理数据，则设置为true；如果处理最后的数据未分块，则设置为false。默认为false。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 206px;">     <h2 id="aspect11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Aspect<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="aspect11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Aspect类用于封装提供切面能力（Aspect Oriented Programming，简写AOP）的接口，这些接口可用于对类方法进行前后插桩或替换实现。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2696px;">     <h3 id="addbefore11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">addBefore<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="addbefore11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static addBefore(targetClass: Object, methodName: string, isStatic: boolean, before: Function): void</p>     <p>在指定的类对象的原方法执行前插入一个函数。执行addBefore接口后，先运行插入的函数逻辑，再执行指定类对象的原方法。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">targetClass</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Object</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的类对象。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">methodName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的原方法名，不支持read-only方法。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">isStatic</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的原方法是否为静态方法。true表示静态方法，false表示实例方法。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">before</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Function</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要插入的函数对象。函数有参数，则第一个参数是this对象（若isStatic为true，则为类对象即targetClass；若isStatic为false，则为调用方法的实例对象），其余参数是原方法的参数。函数也可以无参数，无参时不做处理。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">MyClass</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">msg</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'msg000'</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">arg</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>): <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'foo arg is '</span> + arg);</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">msg</span>;</li><li>  }</li><li>

class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2544px;">     <h3 id="addafter11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">addAfter<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="addafter11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static addAfter(targetClass: Object, methodName: string, isStatic: boolean, after: Function): void</p>     <p>在指定的类方法执行后插入一段逻辑。最终返回插入函数执行后的返回值。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">targetClass</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Object</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的类对象。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">methodName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的原方法名，不支持read-only方法。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">isStatic</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的原方法是否为静态方法。true表示静态方法，false表示实例方法。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">after</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Function</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要插入的函数。函数有参数时，则第一个参数是this对象（若isStatic为true，则为类对象即targetClass；若isStatic为false，则为调用方法的实例对象），第二个参数是原方法的返回值（如果原方法没有返回值，则为undefined），其余参数是原方法的参数。函数也可以无参，无参时不做处理。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">replace<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="replace11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static replace(targetClass: Object, methodName: string, isStatic: boolean, instead: Function) : void</p>     <p>将指定类的原方法替换为另一个函数。replace接口执行完成后，调用指定的类方法时，仅执行替换后的逻辑。最终返回替换函数执行完毕的返回值。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">targetClass</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Object</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的类对象。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">methodName</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的原方法名，不支持read-only方法。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">isStatic</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的原方法是否为静态方法。true表示静态方法，false表示实例方法。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">instead</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Function</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要用来替换原方法的函数。函数有参数时，则第一个参数是this对象（若isStatic为true，则为类对象即targetClass；若isStatic为false，则为调用方法的实例对象），其余参数是原方法的参数。函数也可以无参，无参时不做处理。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> class="hljs-comment">// 输出结果：asp.msg is msg111</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="textdecoder" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">TextDecoder<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textdecoder" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>TextDecoder用于将字节数组解码为字符串，支持utf-8、utf-16le/be、iso-8859和windows-1251等不同的编码格式。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1239px;">     <h3 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> 以下各项对应的系统能力均为SystemCapability.Utils.Lang。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.4.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.4.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.4.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.4.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">encoding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>编码格式。</p>          <p>- 支持格式：utf-8、ibm866、iso-8859-2、iso-8859-3、iso-8859-4、iso-8859-5、iso-8859-6、iso-8859-7、iso-8859-8、iso-8859-8-i、iso-8859-10、iso-8859-13、iso-8859-14、iso-8859-15、koi8-r、koi8-u、macintosh、windows-874、windows-1250、windows-1251、windows-1252、windows-1253、windows-1254、windows-1255、windows-1256、windows-1257、windows-1258、x-mac-cyrillic、gbk、gb18030、big5、euc-jp、iso-2022-jp、shift_jis、euc-kr、utf-16be、utf-16le、gb2312、iso-8859-1。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">fatal</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是否显示致命错误，true表示显示，false表示不显示。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">ignoreBOM</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是否忽略BOM（byte order marker）标记，默认值为false，表示解码结果包含BOM标记。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="encodeintouint8arrayinfo11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">EncodeIntoUint8ArrayInfo<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="encodeintouint8arrayinfo11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 354px;">     <h3 id="属性-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.4.1.6.1.1" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 254px;">     <h2 id="textencoder" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">TextEncoder<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textencoder" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>TextEncoder将字符串编码为字节数组，支持多种编码格式。</p>     <p>在使用TextEncoder进行编码时，需要注意不同编码格式下字符所占的字节数不同。务必明确指定编码格式，以确保编码结果正确。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1005px;">     <h3 id="属性-2" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性-2" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> 以下各项对应的系统能力均为SystemCapability.Utils.Lang。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.4.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.4.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.4.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.4.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">encoding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>编码格式。</p>          <p>- 支持格式：utf-8、gb2312、gb18030、ibm866、iso-8859-1、iso-8859-2、iso-8859-3、iso-8859-4、iso-8859-5、iso-8859-6、iso-8859-7、iso-8859-8、iso-8859-8-i、iso-8859-10、iso-8859-13、iso-8859-14、iso-8859-15、koi8-r、koi8-u、macintosh、windows-874、windows-1250、windows-1251、windows-1252、windows-1253、windows-1254、windows-1255、windows-1256、windows-1257、windows-1258、gbk、big5、euc-jp、iso-2022-jp、shift_jis、euc-kr、x-mac-cyrillic、utf-16be、utf-16le。</p>          <p>- 默认值是：'utf-8'。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 479px;">     <h3 id="getcommonfactor9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getCommonFactor<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static getCommonFactor(number1: number, number2: number): number</p>     <p>获取两个整数的最大公约数。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口要求参数number1和number2必须是整数类型。如果传入的参数是小数类型，不会进行拦截，但是会输出错误信息："getCommonFactor: The type of Parameter must be integer"。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">整数类型。-Number.MAX_VALUE &lt;= number1 &lt;= Number.MAX_VALUE。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">整数类型。-Number.MAX_VALUE &lt;= number2 &lt;= Number.MAX_VALUE。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回两个给定数字的最大公约数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">LRUCache<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="lrucache9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>LRUCache用于在缓存空间不足时，将近期最少使用的数据替换为新数据。此设计基于资源访问的考虑：近期访问的数据，可能在不久的将来会再次访问。因此最少访问的数据被认为价值最低，应当优先从缓存中移除。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 614px;">     <h3 id="属性-3" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性-3" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> 以下各项对应的系统能力均为SystemCapability.Utils.Lang。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.4.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.4.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.4.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.4.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">length</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">updateCapacity<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="updatecapacity9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>updateCapacity(newCapacity: number): void</p>     <p>更新缓冲区容量为指定值，如果newCapacity小于或等于0，则抛出异常。当缓冲区中值的总数大于指定容量时，会执行删除操作。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div id="mcps1.3.62.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">newCapacity</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指示要为缓冲区自定义的容量，最大值不能超过2147483647。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1212px;">     <h3 id="get9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">get<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="get9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>get(key: K): V | undefined</p>     <p>返回键对应的值。当键不在缓冲区中时，通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#createdefault9">createDefault<sup>9+</sup></a>接口创建，若createDefault创建的值不为undefined时，此时会调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#afterremoval9">afterRemoval<sup>9+</sup></a>接口，返回createDefault创建的值。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">K</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要查询的键。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">V | undefined</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果指定的键存在于缓冲区中，则返回与键关联的值；否则返回createDefault创建的值。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1233px;">     <h3 id="put9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">put<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="put9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>put(key: K,value: V): V</p>     <p>将键值对添加到缓冲区，返回与添加的键关联的值。当缓冲区中值的总数超过容量时，执行删除操作。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">K</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要添加的键。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">V</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指示与要添加的键关联的值。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">V</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回与添加的键关联的值。如果键或值为空，则抛出此异常。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p> Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div id="values9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">values<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon V[]</p>     <p>获取当前缓冲区中所有值，从最近最少访问到最近访问的顺序列表。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">remove<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="remove9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>remove(key: K): V | undefined</p>     <p>从当前缓冲区中删除指定的键及其关联的值，并返回键关联的值。如果指定的键不存在，则返回undefined。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">K</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要删除的键值。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.76.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">V | undefined</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回一个包含已删除键值对的Optional对象；如果key不存在，则返回undefined，如果key为null，则抛出异常。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1632px;">     <h3 id="afterremoval9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">afterRemoval<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="afterremoval9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>afterRemoval(isEvict: boolean, key: K, value: V, newValue: V): void</p>     <p>删除值后执行后续操作，这些操作由开发者自行实现。本接口会在删除操作时被调用，如<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#get9">get<sup>9+</sup></a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#put9">put<sup>9+</sup></a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#remove9">remove<sup>9+</sup></a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#clear9">clear<sup>9+</sup></a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#updatecapacity9">updateCapacity<sup>9+</sup></a>接口。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">isEvict</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当因容量不足而调用该方法时，参数值设置为true，其他情况设置为false。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">key</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1740px;">     <h3 id="intersect9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">intersect<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="intersect9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>intersect(range: ScopeHelper): ScopeHelper</p>     <p>获取给定范围和当前范围的交集。当交集为空集时，抛出异常。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1761px;">     <h3 id="intersect9-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">intersect<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="intersect9-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>intersect(lowerObj:ScopeType,upperObj:ScopeType):ScopeHelper</p>     <p>获取当前范围与指定下限和上限范围的交集。当交集为空集时，抛出异常。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p> <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.97.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.97.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#scopetype8">ScopeType</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">如果传入的value小于下限，返回lowerObj；如果大于上限值，返回upperObj；如果在当前范围内，返回value。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 254px;">     <h2 id="base64helper9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Base64Helper<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="base64helper9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Base64Helper类提供Base64编解码和Base64URL编解码功能。Base64编码表包含A-Z、a-z、0-9这62个字符，以及"+"和"/"这两个特殊字符。在编码时，将原始数据按3个字节一组进行划分，得到若干个6位的数字，然后使用Base64编码表中对应的字符来表示这些数字。如果最后剩余1或2个字节，则需要使用"="字符进行补齐。Base64URL编码表包含A-Z、a-z、0-9以及"-"和"_"64个字符，Base64URL编码结果不含"="。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 463px;">     <h3 id="constructor9-5" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">constructor<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="constructor9-5" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>constructor()</p>     <p>Base64Helper的构造函数。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" <h3 id="encodetostringsync9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">encodeToStringSync<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="encodetostringsync9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>encodeToStringSync(src: Uint8Array, options?: Type): string</p>     <p>将输入的Uint8Array字节数组进行Base64编码，返回一个字符串结果。该方法支持多种编码格式，包括标准Base64编码、MIME格式的Base64编码（带有换行符）、URL安全格式的Base64编码等。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">src</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Uint8Array</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">待编码Uint8Array对象。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options<sup>10+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#type10">Type</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>从API version 10开始支持该参数，表示对应的编码格式。</p>          <p>此参数可选，可选值为：util.Type.BASIC，util.Type.MIME，util.Type.BASIC_URL_SAFE 和util.Type.MIME_URL_SAFE，默认值为：util.Type.BASIC。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.BASIC，表示Base64编码，返回值没有回车符、换行符。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.MIME，表示使用Base64编码。如果返回值超过76个字符，则会在每76个字符处进行换行，并以'\r\n'结束每行。如果返回值少于76个字符，则会抛出异常。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.BASIC_URL_SAFE，表示Base64URL编码，返回值没有回车符、换行符。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.MIME_URL_SAFE，表示Base64URL编码，返回值每一行不超过76个字符，而且每行以'\r\n'符结束。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回编码后的字符串。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.101.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-kva-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div   <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.104.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options<sup>10+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-util#type10">Type</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>从API version 10开始支持该参数，表示对应的编码格式。</p>          <p>此参数可选，可选值为：util.Type.BASIC，util.Type.MIME，util.Type.BASIC_URL_SAFE和util.Type.MIME_URL_SAFE，默认值为：util.Type.BASIC。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.BASIC，表示Base64编码，返回值没有回车符、换行符。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.MIME，表示Base64编码，返回值每一行不超过76个字符，而且每行以'\r\n'符结束。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.BASIC_URL_SAFE，表示Base64URL编码，返回值没有回车符、换行符。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.MIME_URL_SAFE，表示Base64URL编码，返回值每一行不超过76个字符，而且每行以'\r\n'符结束。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div <p>此参数可选，可选值为：util.Type.BASIC，util.Type.MIME，util.Type.BASIC_URL_SAFE和util.Type.MIME_URL_SAFE，默认值为：util.Type.BASIC。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.BASIC时，表示Base64解码。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.MIME时，表示Base64解码，src入参包含回车符、换行符。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.BASIC_URL_SAFE，表示Base64URL解码。</p>          <p>- 当参数取值为util.Type.MIME_URL_SAFE，表示Base64URL解码，src入参包含回车符、换行符。</p></td> anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="write12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>write(chunk: string | Uint8Array): string</p>     <p>返回一个解码后的字符串，确保Uint8Array末尾的任何不完整的多字节字符从返回的字符串中被过滤，并保存在一个内部的buffer中用于下次调用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> id="mcps1.3.108.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.108.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.108.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.108.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">chunk</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string | Uint8Array</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">需要解码的字符串。会根据输入的编码类型进行解码，参数为Uint8Array时正常解码，参数为string时会将参数直接返回。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p> width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回解码后的字符串。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>end(chunk?: string | Uint8Array): string</p>     <p>结束解码过程，以字符串形式返回存储在内部缓冲区中的所有剩余输入。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version
